USERMESSAGE #9
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→# priorart
     2→
     3→Prior art scanner for ideas. Searches GitHub repositories and Hacker News discussions to assess how crowded a space is, then produces a **Reality Signal** score (0–100).
     4→
     5→## Installation
     6→
     7→```bash
     8→pip install priorart
     9→```
    10→
    11→Or with `uv`:
    12→
    13→```bash
    14→uv add priorart
    15→```
    16→
    17→## Usage
    18→
    19→```bash
    20→# Basic scan (table output)
    21→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker'
    22→
    23→# JSON output
    24→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --format json
    25→
    26→# Markdown output (same format as GitHub Action comment)
    27→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --format markdown
    28→
    29→# Limit to specific sources
    30→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --sources hn
    31→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --sources github,hn
    32→
    33→# With explicit GitHub token
    34→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --github-token ghp_...
    35→```
    36→
    37→The `GITHUB_TOKEN` environment variable is used automatically if set:
    38→
    39→```bash
    40→export GITHUB_TOKEN=ghp_...
    41→priorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --format json
    42→```
    43→
    44→## Output formats
    45→
    46→### JSON (`--format json`)
    47→
    48→```json
    49→{
    50→  "query": "AI personal finance tracker",
    51→  "queries": ["AI personal finance tracker", "AI personal finance"],
    52→  "sources": [
    53→    {
    54→      "type": "github",
    55→      "results": [
    56→        {
    57→          "name": "org/repo",
    58→          "stars": 1234,
    59→          "description": "...",
    60→          "url": "https://github.com/org/repo",
    61→          "updated": "2024-01-01",
    62→          "language": "Python"
    63→        }
    64→      ]
    65→    },
    66→    {
    67→      "type": "hn",
    68→      "results": [
    69→        {
    70→          "title": "...",
    71→          "points": 42,
    72→          "comments": 17,
    73→          "url": "https://news.ycombinator.com/item?id=...",
    74→          "date": "2024-03-01"
    75→        }
    76→      ]
    77→    }
    78→  ],
    79→  "signal": {
    80→    "score": 45,
    81→    "verdict": "MODERATE",
    82→    "breakdown": {
    83→      "github": 30,
    84→      "hn": 15
    85→    }
    86→  },
    87→  "meta": {
    88→    "timestamp": "2026-03-07T00:00:00+00:00",
    89→    "version": "0.1.0"
    90→  }
    91→}
    92→```
    93→
    94→### Markdown (`--format markdown`)
    95→
    96→Produces the same Markdown comment format used by the `prior-art-scan` GitHub Action.
    97→
    98→### Table (`--format table`)
    99→
   100→Plain-text table for terminal output (default).
   101→
   102→## Reality Signal
   103→
   104→The Reality Signal (0–100) reflects how crowded the solution space is:
   105→
   106→| Score | Verdict | Meaning |
   107→|-------|---------|---------|
   108→| 0–29 | 🟢 LOW | Greenfield opportunity or underserved niche |
   109→| 30–60 | 🟡 MODERATE | Some existing solutions, differentiation needed |
   110→| 61–100 | 🔴 HIGH | Crowded space, needs strong differentiator |
   111→
   112→The score is composed of:
   113→- **GitHub component (0–60):** number of repos found + max star count
   114→- **HN component (0–40):** number of discussions found + max point count
   115→
   116→## Development
   117→
   118→```bash
   119→# Install with dev dependencies
   120→pip install -e ".[dev]"
   121→
   122→# Run tests
   123→pytest
   124→
   125→# Lint
   126→ruff check src tests
   127→```
   128→
   129→## Package structure
   130→
   131→```
   132→src/priorart/
   133→├── __init__.py       # version
   134→├── scanner.py        # orchestrator + query builder
   135→├── scoring.py        # reality signal computation
   136→├── formatters.py     # JSON, markdown, table output
   137→├── cli.py            # typer CLI entry point
   138→└── sources/
   139→    ├── __init__.py
   140→    ├── github.py     # GitHub repository search
   141→    └── hn.py         # Hacker News search (Algolia API)
   142→```
   143→

     1→"""Orchestrator — builds queries, runs sources, computes signal."""

     3→from __future__ import annotations

     5→import re
     6→import sys
     7→import time
     8→from datetime import datetime, timezone
     9→
    10→from priorart import __version__
    11→from priorart.scoring import compute_signal
    12→from priorart.sources.github import search_repos
    13→from priorart.sources.hn import search_discussions
    14→
    15→
    16→def _result_text(item: dict, kind: str) -> str:
    17→    """Extract a single text string to embed from a result item."""
    18→    if kind == "repo":
    19→        name = item.get("name") or ""
    20→        desc = item.get("description") or ""
    21→        return f"{name} {desc}".strip()
    22→    # hn
    23→    return item.get("title") or ""
    24→
    25→
    26→def build_queries(title: str, body: str = "") -> list[str]:
    27→    """Build search queries from the idea title (and optional body).
    28→
    29→    Uses the title directly plus cleaned variants.
    30→    The title IS the idea description — no LLM needed.
    31→    """
    32→    clean = title.strip()
    33→    for prefix in ["idea:", "idea -", "[idea]"]:
    34→        if clean.lower().startswith(prefix):
    35→            clean = clean[len(prefix) :].strip()
    36→
    37→    queries: list[str] = []
    38→    seen: set[str] = set()
    39→
    40→    def add(q: str) -> None:
    41→        q = q.strip()
    42→        if q and q.lower() not in seen:
    43→            seen.add(q.lower())
    44→            queries.append(q)
    45→
    46→    # Split on common separators
    47→    parts = [clean]
    48→    for sep in [" — ", " - ", " – ", " | "]:
    49→        if sep in clean:
    50→            parts = [p.strip() for p in clean.split(sep) if p.strip()]
    51→            break
    52→
    53→    for part in parts:
    54→        stripped = re.sub(r"\([^)]*\)", "", part).strip()
    55→        stripped = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", " ", stripped).strip()
    56→        stripped = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", stripped)
    57→        if stripped:
    58→            if len(stripped.split()) <= 1 and len(parts) > 1:
    59→                continue
    60→            add(stripped)
    61→
    62→    full = " ".join(queries)
    63→    words = full.split()
    64→    if len(words) > 5:
    65→        add(" ".join(words[:5]))
    66→        add(" ".join(words[:3]))
    67→
    68→    if body:
    69→        for line in body.split("
"):
    70→            line = line.strip().strip("#").strip("-").strip("*").strip()
    71→            if len(line) > 10 and not line.startswith(("http", "![", "<!--")):
    72→                body_clean = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", " ", line).strip()
    73→                body_clean = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", body_clean)
    74→                body_words = body_clean.split()
    75→                if len(body_words) >= 3:
    76→                    add(" ".join(body_words[:6]))
    77→                    break
    78→
    79→    return queries
    80→
    81→
    82→def scan(
    83→    idea: str,
    84→    github_token: str | None = None,
    85→    sources: list[str] | None = None,
    86→    body: str = "",
    87→    openai_key: str | None = None,
    88→) -> dict:
    89→    """Run a full prior-art scan and return structured results.
    90→
    91→    Args:
    92→        idea: The idea description to scan.
    93→        github_token: GitHub personal access token (required for GitHub source).
    94→        sources: List of source names to query. Defaults to ["github", "hn"].
    95→        body: Optional body text for additional query extraction.
    96→        openai_key: OpenAI API key. When provided, results are reranked by
    97→            cosine similarity to the idea embedding and the signal score
    98→            incorporates a semantic component.
    99→
   100→    Returns:
   101→        Structured dict: {query, queries, sources, signal, meta}
   102→    """
   103→    if sources is None:
   104→        sources = ["github", "hn"]
   105→
   106→    queries = build_queries(idea, body)
   107→
   108→    all_repos: list[dict] = []
   109→    all_hn: list[dict] = []
   110→    seen_repo_names: set[str] = set()
   111→    seen_hn_urls: set[str] = set()
   112→
   113→    for query in queries:
   114→        if "github" in sources:
   115→            repos = search_repos(query, github_token)
   116→            for r in repos:
   117→                if r["name"] not in seen_repo_names:
   118→                    seen_repo_names.add(r["name"])
   119→                    all_repos.append(r)
   120→            time.sleep(1)
   121→
   122→        if "hn" in sources:
   123→            hn = search_discussions(query)
   124→            for h in hn:
   125→                if h["url"] not in seen_hn_urls:
   126→                    seen_hn_urls.add(h["url"])
   127→                    all_hn.append(h)
   128→            time.sleep(0.5)
   129→
   130→    all_repos.sort(key=lambda r: r["stars"], reverse=True)
   131→    all_hn.sort(key=lambda h: h["points"], reverse=True)
   132→
   133→    # Semantic reranking — only when an OpenAI key is supplied and there are results
   134→    top_similarity: float | None = None
   135→    if openai_key and (all_repos or all_hn):
   136→        try:
   137→            from priorart.embeddings import embed_texts, rank_by_similarity
   138→
   139→            repo_texts = [_result_text(r, "repo") for r in all_repos]
   140→            hn_texts = [_result_text(h, "hn") for h in all_hn]
   141→            all_texts = [idea] + repo_texts + hn_texts
   142→
   143→            embeddings = embed_texts(all_texts, openai_key)
   144→            query_vec = embeddings[0]
   145→            repo_embeddings = embeddings[1 : len(all_repos) + 1]
   146→            hn_embeddings = embeddings[len(all_repos) + 1 :]
   147→
   148→            if all_repos:
   149→                all_repos = rank_by_similarity(query_vec, all_repos, repo_embeddings)
   150→            if all_hn:
   151→                all_hn = rank_by_similarity(query_vec, all_hn, hn_embeddings)
   152→
   153→            # Average similarity of top-3 across both sources
   154→            top_sims = (
   155→                [r["similarity"] for r in all_repos[:3]]
   156→                + [h["similarity"] for h in all_hn[:3]]
   157→            )
   158→            if top_sims:
   159→                top_similarity = sum(top_sims) / len(top_sims)
   160→        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   161→            print(f"Warning: semantic reranking failed ({exc})", file=sys.stderr)
   162→
   163→    signal = compute_signal(all_repos, all_hn, top_similarity)
   164→
   165→    source_results = []
   166→    if "github" in sources:
   167→        source_results.append({"type": "github", "results": all_repos})
   168→    if "hn" in sources:
   169→        source_results.append({"type": "hn", "results": all_hn})
   170→
   171→    return {
   172→        "query": idea,
   173→        "queries": queries,
   174→        "sources": source_results,
   175→        "signal": signal,
   176→        "meta": {
   177→            "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
   178→            "version": __version__,
   179→        },
   180→    }
   181→

   110→        token="fake-token",

   112→        repos=None,
   113→        hn=None,

   180→    def test_deduplicates_repos_by_name(self):
   181→        shared = {**_MOCK_REPO, "name": "org/shared"}
   182→        unique = {**_MOCK_REPO, "name": "org/unique"}
   183→        call_n = [0]
   184→
   185→        def _repos(query, token, **kw):
   186→            call_n[0] += 1
   187→            return [shared] if call_n[0] == 1 else [shared, unique]

   189→        # Use a long title so build_queries produces 2+ queries
   190→        with patch("priorart.scanner.search_repos", side_effect=_repos):
   191→            with patch("priorart.scanner.search_discussions", return_value=[]):

   220→    def test_repos_sorted_by_stars_descending(self):
   221→        low = {**_MOCK_REPO, "name": "org/low", "stars": 10}
   222→        high = {**_MOCK_REPO, "name": "org/high", "stars": 1000}
   223→        result = self._scan(repos=[low, high])
   224→        gh = next(s["results"] for s in result["sources"] if s["type"] == "github")
   225→        stars = [r["stars"] for r in gh]
   226→        assert stars == sorted(stars, reverse=True)

   239→        result = self._scan(hn=[low, high], token=None, sources=["hn"])
   240→        hn = next(s["results"] for s in result["sources"] if s["type"] == "hn")
   241→        pts = [r["points"] for r in hn]
   242→        assert pts == sorted(pts, reverse=True)

   305→def _fake_embed_texts(texts, api_key):
   306→    """Return deterministic unit vectors: text at index i → e_i."""
   307→    vecs = []
   308→    for i, _ in enumerate(texts):
   309→        v = [0.0] * len(texts)
   310→        v[i] = 1.0
   311→        vecs.append(v)
   312→    return vecs
   313→

     1→"""GitHub repository search source."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→import sys
     6→
     7→import httpx
     8→
     9→GITHUB_API = "https://api.github.com"
    10→
    11→
    12→def search_repos(
    13→    query: str,
    14→    token: str | None = None,
    15→    max_results: int = 10,
    16→) -> list[dict]:
    17→    """Search GitHub for repositories matching the query."""
    18→    headers = {
    19→        "Accept": "application/vnd.github+json",
    20→        "X-GitHub-Api-Version": "2022-11-28",
    21→    }
    22→    if token:
    23→        headers["Authorization"] = f"Bearer {token}"
    24→    url = f"{GITHUB_API}/search/repositories"
    25→    params = {
    26→        "q": query,
    27→        "sort": "stars",
    28→        "order": "desc",
    29→        "per_page": max_results,
    30→    }
    31→    try:
    32→        resp = httpx.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=15)
    33→        resp.raise_for_status()
    34→        data = resp.json()
    35→        return [
    36→            {
    37→                "name": r["full_name"],
    38→                "stars": r["stargazers_count"],
    39→                "description": (r.get("description") or "")[:120],
    40→                "url": r["html_url"],
    41→                "updated": r["updated_at"][:10],
    42→                "language": r.get("language") or "—",
    43→            }
    44→            for r in data.get("items", [])[:max_results]
    45→        ]
    46→    except Exception as e:
    47→        print(f"GitHub search failed for '{query}': {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    48→        return []
    49→

     1→"""Hacker News search source via Algolia API."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→import sys
     6→
     7→import httpx
     8→
     9→HN_API = "https://hn.algolia.com/api/v1"
    10→
    11→
    12→def search_discussions(
    13→    query: str,
    14→    max_results: int = 5,
    15→) -> list[dict]:
    16→    """Search Hacker News for discussions matching the query."""
    17→    url = f"{HN_API}/search"
    18→    params = {
    19→        "query": query,
    20→        "tags": "story",
    21→        "hitsPerPage": max_results,
    22→        "numericFilters": "points>5",
    23→    }
    24→    try:
    25→        resp = httpx.get(url, params=params, timeout=15)
    26→        resp.raise_for_status()
    27→        data = resp.json()
    28→        return [
    29→            {
    30→                "title": h["title"],
    31→                "points": h.get("points", 0),
    32→                "comments": h.get("num_comments", 0),
    33→                "url": f"https://news.ycombinator.com/item?id={h['objectID']}",
    34→                "date": h.get("created_at", "")[:10],
    35→            }
    36→            for h in data.get("hits", [])[:max_results]
    37→        ]
    38→    except Exception as e:
    39→        print(f"HN search failed for '{query}': {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    40→        return []

search_discussions\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Concept-based query expansion helpers\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n# Leading tokens that signal \"tech flavour\" rather than the core domain concept.\n# Stored as normalised forms: lowercase, non-alpha characters removed.\n_TECH_PREFIX_NORMS: frozenset[str] = frozenset({\n    # AI / ML abbreviations\n    \"ai\", \"ml\", \"llm\", \"gpt\",\n    # Compound AI descriptors (normalised: hyphens/spaces removed)\n    \"aipowered\", \"mlpowered\", \"llmpowered\", \"aidriven\", \"aiassisted\",\n    # Deployment / hosting descriptors\n    \"selfhosted\", \"opensource\", search synonym.\n# Only the first matching word in a phrase is swapped, producing one variant.\n_PRODUCT_SYNONYMS: dict[str, str] = {\n    \"tracker\": \"monitor\",\n    \"monitor\": \"tracker\",\n    \"tracking\": \"monitoring\",\n    \"monitoring\": \"tracking\",\n    \"manager\": \"organizer\",\n    \"management\": \"platform\",\n    \"analyzer\": \"inspector\",\n    \"analysis\": \"scanner\",\n    \"optimizer\": \"analyzer\",\n    \"aggregator\": \"hub\",\n    \"alerting\": \"monitoring\",\n    \"notifier\": \"alerter\",\n}\n\n\ndef _norm_word(w: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Return *w* lowercased with all non-alpha characters removed.\"\"\"\n    return re.sub(r\"[^a-z]\", \"\", w.lower())\n\n\ndef _strip_tech_prefix(phrase: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Remove leading tech-buzzword tokens from *phrase*.\n\n    Examples::\n\n        \"AI personal finance tracker\"  -> \"personal finance tracker\"\n        \"Self-hosted uptime monitor\"   -> \"uptime monitor\"\n        \"Smart home hub\"               -> \"home hub\"\n        \"normal idea\"                  -> \"normal idea\"  (unchanged)\n    \"\"\"\n    words = phrase.split()\n    i = 0\n    while i < len(words) and _norm_word(words[i]) in _TECH_PREFIX_NORMS:\n        i += 1\n    return \" \".join(words[i:])\n\n\ndef _synonym_variant(phrase: str) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Return *phrase* with the first product-type word replaced by its synonym.\n\n    Returns ``None`` if no known product-type word is found.\n    \"\"\"\n    words = phrase.split()\n    for i, word in enumerate(words):\n        key = _norm_word(word)\n        if key in _PRODUCT_SYNONYMS:\n            return \" \".join(words[:i] + [_PRODUCT_SYNONYMS[key]] + words[i + 1:])\n    return None\n\n\ndef _result_text(item: dict, kind: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Extract a single text string to embed from a result item.\"\"\"\n    if kind == \"repo\":\n        name = item.get(\"name\") or \"\"\n        desc = item.get(\"description\") or \"\"\n        return f\"{name} {desc}\".strip()\n    # hn\n    return item.get(\"title\") or \"\"\n\n\ndef build_queries(title: str, body: str = \"\") -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Build search queries from the idea title (and optional body).\n\n    Generates multiple search angles:\n    - The title itself (possibly split on separators)\n    - Truncated variants for long titles\n    - A tech-buzzword-stripped variant exposing the core domain concept\n    - A synonym variant replacing common product-type words\n    - An optional query extracted from the body text\n    \"\"\"\n    clean = title.strip()\n    for prefix in [\"idea:\", \"idea -\", \"[idea]\"]:\n        if clean.lower().startswith(prefix):\n            clean = clean[len(prefix) :].strip()\n\n    queries: list[str] # Split on common separators\n    parts = [clean]\n    for sep in [\" \u2014 \", \" - \", \" \u2013 \", \" | \"]:\n        if sep in clean:\n            parts = [p.strip() for p in clean.split(sep) if p.strip()]\n            break\n\n    for part in parts:\n        stripped = re.sub(r\"\\([^)]*\\)\", \"\", part).strip()\n        stripped = re.sub(r\"[^\\w\\s-]\", \" \", stripped).strip()\n        stripped = re.sub(r\"\\s+\", \" \", stripped)\n        if stripped:\n            if len(stripped.split()) <= 1 and len(parts) > 1:\n                continue\n            add(stripped)\n\n    full = \" \".join(queries)\n    words = full.split()\n    if len(words) > 5:\n        add(\" \".join(words[:5]))\n        add(\" \".join(words[:3]))\n\n    # --- Concept-based search angles ---\n    # Applied to the first (primary) query to keep the total count bounded.\n    if queries:\n        primary = queries[0]\n\n        # 1. Strip leading tech-buzzwords to expose the core domain concept,\n        #    allowing searches to surface results that don't use AI/ML jargon.\n        core = _strip_tech_prefix(primary)\n        if core and core.lower() != primary.lower() and len(core.split()) >= 2:\n            add(core)\n\n        # 2. Replace the first product-type word with a synonym so searches\n        #    cover alternative vocabulary (e.g. \"tracker\" vs \"monitor\").\n        syn = _synonym_variant(primary)\n        if syn:\n            add(syn)\n\n    if body:\n        for line in body.split(\"\\n\"):\n            line = line.strip().strip(\"#\").strip(\"-\").strip(\"*\").strip()\n            if len(line) > 10 and not line.startswith((\"http\", \"![\", \"<!--\")):\n                body_clean = re.sub(r\"[^\\w\\s-]\", \" \", line).strip()\n                body_clean = re.sub(r\"\\s+\", \" \", body_clean)\n                body_words = body_clean.split()\n                if len(body_words) >= 3:\n                    add(\" \".join(body_words[:6]))\n                    break\n\n    return queries"

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #68
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/priorart/scanner.py` — Added `_TECH_PREFIX_NORMS`, `_PRODUCT_SYNONYMS` constants and `_norm_word()`, `_strip_tech_prefix()`, `_synonym_variant()` helpers; updated `build_queries()` to append up to 2 concept-variant queries (tech-stripped core + product-word synonym) for the primary query - `tests/test_scanner.py` — Added `TestBuildQueriesConceptVariants` class with 13 new tests covering AI/LLM/Smart/Self-hosted prefix stripping, synonym variants, deduplication, and edge cases ## Key Decisions - Applied concept variants only to the first (primary) query, not all base queries — keeps total query count bounded (max +2) and avoids excessive API calls/sleep time - Single-word core concepts (after stripping) are silently skipped — a standalone "tracker" query would be too noisy - One synonym per query (first matching product-type word) rather than all possible combinations — diversity without explosion ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-256-smarter-query-generation` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/priorart/pull/4
